   <h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">
    List of
    <i>
     Dexter
    </i>
    episodes
   </h1>
   <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">
    <div id="siteSub">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div>
    <div id="contentSub">
    </div>
    <div class="mw-jump" id="jump-to-nav">
     Jump to:
     <a href="#mw-head">
      navigation
     </a>
     ,
     <a href="#p-search">
      search
     </a>
    </div>
    <div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en">
     <div class="floatright">
      <a href="/wiki/Dexter_(TV_series)" title="Dexter (TV series)">
       <img alt="Dexter Logo.svg" data-file-height="1034" data-file-width="1352" height="191" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Dexter_Logo.svg/250px-Dexter_Logo.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Dexter_Logo.svg/375px-Dexter_Logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/bd/Dexter_Logo.svg/500px-Dexter_Logo.svg.png 2x" width="250"/>
      </a>
     </div>
     <p>
      <i>
       <a href="/wiki/Dexter_(TV_series)" title="Dexter (TV series)">
        Dexter
       </a>
      </i>
      is an American television drama that was broadcast on the premium cable channel
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Showtime_(TV_channel)" title="Showtime (TV channel)">
       Showtime
      </a>
      from October 1, 2006 to September 22, 2013.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-1">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        1
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      A total of 96 episodes of
      <i>
       Dexter
      </i>
      were broadcast over eight seasons. The series is based on characters created by
      <a href="/wiki/Jeff_Lindsay_(writer)" title="Jeff Lindsay (writer)">
       Jeff Lindsay
      </a>
      for his
      <a href="/wiki/Darkly_Dreaming_Dexter" title="Darkly Dreaming Dexter">
       "Dexter" series of novels
      </a>
      . The series follows the life of
      <a href="/wiki/Dexter_Morgan" title="Dexter Morgan">
       Dexter Morgan
      </a>
      (
      <a href="/wiki/Michael_C._Hall" title="Michael C. Hall">
       Michael C. Hall
      </a>
      ), a Miami Metro Police Department
      <a href="/wiki/Bloodstain_pattern_analysis" title="Bloodstain pattern analysis">
       blood pattern analyst
      </a>
      with a double life.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pilot_2-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-pilot-2">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        2
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      While investigating murders in the homicide division, Dexter hunts and kills murderers and criminals who have escaped the justice system.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pilot_2-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-pilot-2">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        2
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Although the first season is based on the events of
      <i>
       <a href="/wiki/Darkly_Dreaming_Dexter" title="Darkly Dreaming Dexter">
        Darkly Dreaming Dexter
       </a>
      </i>
      , the series' subsequent seasons do not follow the novels in the series.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IGNs2_3-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-IGNs2-3">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        3
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Departing from the narrative of Lindsay's second Dexter novel
      <i>
       <a href="/wiki/Dearly_Devoted_Dexter" title="Dearly Devoted Dexter">
        Dearly Devoted Dexter
       </a>
      </i>
      , the show's writer
      <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Cerone" title="Daniel Cerone">
       Daniel Cerone
      </a>
      said that the writers "didn't see the opportunity in the second book" to adapt it.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-IGNs2_3-1">
       <a href="#cite_note-IGNs2-3">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        3
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      The series has received generally favorable reviews from critics, while the second season received universal acclaim.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-metacritic_4-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-metacritic-4">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        4
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      The
      <a href="/wiki/Dexter_(episode)" title="Dexter (episode)">
       pilot episode
      </a>
      , which aired in the USA on October 1, 2006, attracted more than a million viewers, giving Showtime its highest series
      <a href="/wiki/Nielsen_ratings" title="Nielsen ratings">
       ratings
      </a>
      in nearly two years.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-pilotratings_5-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-pilotratings-5">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        5
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Encouraged by its critical success and high ratings,
      <a href="/wiki/CBS" title="CBS">
       CBS
      </a>
      began broadcasting
      <i>
       Dexter
      </i>
      for
      <a href="/wiki/Free-to-air" title="Free-to-air">
       free-to-air
      </a>
      on February 17, 2008,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-latimes1_6-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-latimes1-6">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        6
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      thus making
      <i>
       Dexter
      </i>
      the first program in two decades to air on a national broadcast network after being shown on a premium cable channel.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nytimes1_7-0">
       <a href="#cite_note-nytimes1-7">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        7
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Eight seasons comprising twelve episodes each have been broadcast in the United States and abroad.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8">
       <a href="#cite_note-8">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        8
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      All eight seasons have been released on DVD and on Blu-ray; box sets containing the first three seasons were released on August 18, 2009, on both DVD
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9">
       <a href="#cite_note-9">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        9
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      and Blu-ray.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10">
       <a href="#cite_note-10">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        10
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <p>
      The show received
      <a href="/wiki/List_of_awards_and_nominations_received_by_Dexter_(TV_series)" title="List of awards and nominations received by Dexter (TV series)">
       multiple nominations
      </a>
      for various awards, winning 19including two
      <a href="/wiki/Primetime_Emmy_Award" title="Primetime Emmy Award">
       Primetime Emmy Awards
      </a>
      ,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11">
       <a href="#cite_note-11">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        11
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      two
      <a href="/wiki/Golden_Globe_Award" title="Golden Globe Award">
       Golden Globe Awards
      </a>
      ,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12">
       <a href="#cite_note-12">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        12
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      seven
      <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Satellite_Award" title="Satellite Award">
       Satellite Awards
      </a>
      ,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13">
       <a href="#cite_note-13">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        13
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14">
       <a href="#cite_note-14">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        14
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15">
       <a href="#cite_note-15">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        15
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      five
      <a href="/wiki/Saturn_Award" title="Saturn Award">
       Saturn Awards
      </a>
      ,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16">
       <a href="#cite_note-16">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        16
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      one
      <a href="/wiki/Screen_Actors_Guild_Award" title="Screen Actors Guild Award">
       Screen Actors Guild Award
      </a>
      ,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17">
       <a href="#cite_note-17">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        17
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      and one
      <a href="/wiki/TCA_Awards" title="TCA Awards">
       TCA Award
      </a>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18">
       <a href="#cite_note-18">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        18
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      and was twice selected by the
      <a href="/wiki/American_Film_Institute" title="American Film Institute">
       American Film Institute
      </a>
      as one of the ten best television programs of the year in 2006 and 2007.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19">
       <a href="#cite_note-19">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        19
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20">
       <a href="#cite_note-20">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        20
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Other nominations include
      <a href="/wiki/Producers_Guild_of_America" title="Producers Guild of America">
       PGA Awards
      </a>
      ,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21">
       <a href="#cite_note-21">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        21
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <a href="/wiki/Writers_Guild_of_America_Award" title="Writers Guild of America Award">
       WGA Awards
      </a>
      ,
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22">
       <a href="#cite_note-22">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        22
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      and
      <a href="/wiki/Peabody_Award" title="Peabody Award">
       Peabody Awards
      </a>
      .
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23">
       <a href="#cite_note-23">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        23
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      As of May 2012, the show has been nominated for over 125 awards, 32 of them for Hall for playing the title character.
     </p>
     <p>
     </p>

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Series_overview">
       Series overview
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Dexter_episodes&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Series overview">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <table class="wikitable" style="text-align:center;">
      <caption>
       Seasons of
       <i>
        Dexter
       </i>
      </caption>
      <tr>
       <th colspan="2" rowspan="2" scope="col" style="padding: 0px 8px">
        Season
       </th>
       <th rowspan="2" scope="col" style="padding: 0px 8px">
        Episodes
       </th>
       <th colspan="2" scope="col" style="padding: 0px 8px">
        Originally aired
       </th>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <th scope="col" style="padding: 0px 8px">
        First aired
       </th>
       <th scope="col" style="padding: 0px 8px">

       </th>
      </tr>
      <tr>
       <td style="background:#CC0000;">
       </td>
       <td scope="row">
        <a href="#Season_1_.282006.29">
         1
        </a>
       </td>
       <td>
        12

     <h2>
      <span class="mw-headline" id="Dexter:_Early_Cuts">
       <i>
        Dexter: Early Cuts
       </i>
      </span>
      <span class="mw-editsection">
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        [
       </span>
       <a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_Dexter_episodes&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Dexter: Early Cuts">
        edit
       </a>
       <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
        ]
       </span>
      </span>
     </h2>
     <p>
      In 2009, Showtime started releasing an animated Dexter webseries.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-95">
       <a href="#cite_note-95">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        95
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-96">
       <a href="#cite_note-96">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        96
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      Each story is told in several two-minute chapters, the first three of which were written by series writer and producer
      <a href="/wiki/Lauren_Gussis" title="Lauren Gussis">
       Lauren Gussis
      </a>
      , and premiered in 2009.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-97">
       <a href="#cite_note-97">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        97
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-98">
       <a href="#cite_note-98">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        98
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      More episodes were released in 2010 and 2011.
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-99">
       <a href="#cite_note-99">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        99
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
      <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-100">
       <a href="#cite_note-100">
        <span>
         [
        </span>
        100
        <span>
         ]
        </span>
       </a>
      </sup>
     </p>
     <table class="wikitable plainrowheaders" style="width:100%;">
